The air conditioner in the room was not cooling, and the temperature difference between the inside and outside was huge. The room was extremely hot. I had to turn off the air conditioner to sleep. It was very stuffy. It was cold in the middle of the night and I covered myself with a quilt. When I put it on, I woke up again because of the heat. It was very bad. There was no solution to the problem with the hotel. Way, it was said that the air conditioner was not turned on because of the cold season. The small refrigerator was not replenished, and there was a vacuum cleaner at the door in broad daylight. The intercontinental guest room requirements were completely invisible here. There are very few breakfast options, but the service attitude in the restaurant is great, which is the second highlight. In short, if you bring children, don't stay in this hotel, it is very unfriendly to children.

msg:After roughly reading the negative reviews left by other people on Ctrip, I think they are basically objective, but subjectively some people can accept them and some people don't care. For example, after a hotel has been open for so many years, it is inevitable that the equipment will age, which will lead to a decline in the stay experience and a lower rating. This is not an isolated phenomenon, but it is acceptable.
Perhaps due to limited space and the positioning of a boutique hotel, the entire hotel layout is somewhat cramped. Three meals, afternoon tea and a very simple meal were all in the same restaurant, but the food was pretty good. Some staff seem to be poorly trained and stuck at guest house level. The gym is too small and unattended.
The equipment in the room is aging to varying degrees, but it is still within an acceptable range. I saw in the reviews that there is a distinct smell of sewerage when the toilet lid is lifted, and I also encountered it.
The biggest advantage is the invincible view of Gulangyu Island. Because of the hotel's location, no matter whether its brand is Indigo or not, you can stay in its view room. The Conrad next to it has a diagonal view of Gulangyu Island, and the price is much higher.

Overall, this is my first time staying at Indigo. When I choose a hotel in other cities in the future, I may not choose Indigo unless there is a classic landscape like Gulangyu Island at the door.

It does not meet the five-star standard. I have stayed at a resort hotel on Huandao Road before. The price is similar, but the comfort, luxury and breakfast are very different.
There is no time to use the afternoon tea included in the package. Overall, the price/performance ratio is average. If you consider travel convenience, there are many hotels around to choose from.

msg:The charm of sea view rooms
I experienced an unparalleled charm in my sea view room at Hotel Indigo.
The hotel is located on Lujiang Road, with an excellent geographical location (opposite Gulangyu Island), convenient transportation and beautiful surrounding environment. From the window of the guest room, you can enjoy the magnificent sea view, the Bagua Tower in Gulangyu Island, the statue of Grandpa Zheng Chenggong, the beach outside Shuzhuang Garden, and the Sunlight Rock, the landmark building of Gulangyu Island. Facing Gulangyu Island in the guest room with a pot of tea is simply amazing. .
The facilities in the sea view rooms are very luxurious, the bedding is comfortable, and the bathrooms are spacious and clean. The room is also equipped with various conveniences, such as ear-mounted coffee pods, mini refrigerators, etc., showing the quality and details of a five-star hotel.
The hotel staff are very warm and considerate, especially Xiaogang and Xiaoqin at the front desk, who provide a full range of services from check-in to check-out. The room cleaning was also very timely and made people feel very comfortable.
The hotel's restaurant offers a variety of delicious food, and the taste is very good. The breakfast is also very rich. The Shacha noodles have a rich soup, and the freshly made flat food is served with sea**** and dried shrimps.
Although this hotel is a five-star hotel, the prices are very reasonable. Compared with other hotels of the same level, the price/performance ratio is very high.
All in all, I was very impressed with my stay in the sea view room. Whether it is in terms of facilities, services or catering, I am very satisfied. If you want to enjoy a luxurious accommodation experience in Xiamen, this five-star hotel is definitely a good choice.
